  {
    "name": "slot",
    "type": "HTML",
    "values": {
      "default": "",
      "value": [
        "<div>Elemento 1</div><div>Elemento 2</div><div>Elemento 3</div>"
      ]
    }
  }
]
events: []
description:A virtual scroller component for rendering large lists efficiently. It only renders the visible items in the viewport, improving performance for long lists. Open the devtools and inspect the component, you will see that only the visible items are rendered. And even though it is "loading" with 10,000 elements and images, the DOM does not overload or take long to load
sidebar_label: z-vscroller

import {WcWrapper} from '@site/src/components/WcWrapper/WcWrapper';
import { DocLayout } from '@site/src/components/layouts/DocLayout'


<DocLayout>
# z-vscroller

A virtual scroller component for rendering large lists efficiently. It only renders the visible items in the viewport, improving performance for long lists. Open the devtools and inspect the component, you will see that only the visible items are rendered.
And even though it is "loading" with 10,000 elements and images, the DOM does not overload or take long to load

## Properties

| Prop Name   | Type   | Default Value  | Other Values                    |
|-------------|--------|----------------|---------------------------------|
| `slot` | `HTML` | `None` | `<div>Element 1</div><div>Element 2</div><div>Element 3</div> ... <div>Element 1000</div> ` |

## Events
`none`

## CSS Parts

You can controll the size of the vs-scroller using simple CSS like that:

```css
  z-vscroller {
    width: 500px;
    height: 500px;
  }
```

> ***IMPORTANT!***
> It would not be correct to use variable units such as: '%', 'vh', 'dvh' in the height.



| Part name  | Description                             | 
|--------------|-----------------------------------------|
| `inner` | The main container. Here the items are rendered. | 
| `item` | The individual items within the scroller. | 

--- 

## Examples of use



    ```html
<z-vscroller></z-vscroller>

<z-vscroller>
  <div>Element 1</div>
  <div>Element 2</div>
  <div>Element 3</div>
  <!-- ... -->
  <div>Element 10000</div>
</z-vscroller>

<z-vscroller>
  <p>
    Lorem ipsum, dolor sit amet consectetur adipisicing elit. Consequatur odio
    voluptatum dolores facere non. Magni molestias fuga quis magnam optio,
    consectetur in repellendus corporis eum omnis voluptatibus autem commodi
    sunt.
  </p>
  <img src="https://cdn2.thecatapi.com/images/cdq.png" alt="" />
  <p>
    Lorem ipsum, dolor sit amet consectetur adipisicing elit. Consequatur odio
    voluptatum dolores facere non. Magni molestias fuga quis magnam optio,
    consectetur in repellendus corporis eum omnis voluptatibus autem commodi
    sunt.
  </p>
    <img src="https://cdn2.thecatapi.com/images/XFhRpYS_D.jpg" alt="" />
    <img src="https://cdn2.thecatapi.com/images/a6k.jpg" alt="" />
</z-vscroller>

```
